    1192             : // Allocates a new CallObject.
    1193             : //
    1194             : // This instruction generates two possible instruction sets:
    1195             : //   (1) If the call object is extensible, this is a callVM to create the
    1196             : //       call object.

    6946             : // Store a typed value to an object's dslots or a slots vector. This has a
    6947             : // few advantages over LStoreSlotV:
    6948             : // 1) We can bypass storing the type tag if the slot has the same type as
    6949             : //    the value.
    6950             : // 2) Better register allocation: we can store constants and FP regs directly
    6951             : //    without requiring a second register for the value.

    6953             : {
    6954             :   public:

    6956             :
